1)  
Cheon Seung-il  
As you all know, today is the day we commemorate 'Cheon Seung-il.' On this morning, marking the second anniversary, I would like to briefly speak about the content of 'Cheon Seung-il.'  
The foundation on which the ideal of creation should be realized has been overturned by the Fall.  
If God's original ideal of creation had been realized, the suffering of humanity today, or what we refer to in the Unification Church as the history of indemnity, would not have existed in human history. Had there been no history of indemnity, the family of Adam would have become the center of heaven and earth today, and the history they left behind would have become the cultural history of humanity. The traditions they left would have undoubtedly become the foundation of our lives, moving everything in our daily lives. However, this entire foundation, which should have realized God's ideal of creation, was overturned by the Fall of humanity's ancestors.  
Therefore, according to God's will of salvation providence, we have been working through history to restore what has been overturned. While the family of Adam was responsible for this work, we must recognize that countless people, connected by blood to the family of Adam, from families to tribes, nations, and the world, are all bearing a common destiny and remain in the realm of the Fall today.  
October 4, 1978 (Wed), Headquarters Church.  
* This message was also published in the December 1978 issue of <Unification World>.  
8   Cheon Seung-il  
So, who is the central being of the realm of the Fall, in other words, who is the central being that guides this world? It is not God but Satan. Therefore, all of humanity, as well as the world of existence that is dominated by this being, is under the dominion of Satan. Consequently, all beings within that dominion are in the realm of lamentation. In other words, we understand that they are in a history of resentment, hoping for the day when they can find a time of hope and be liberated again.  
So, what happened because of the Fall? If there had been no Fall, it would have started from the day of God's victory. The perfection of Adam and Eve is the perfection of heaven and earth, the perfection of the world, and the perfection of the nation, tribe, people, and family as a whole. This could have started with one core, but because of the Fall, through a long period, we must reverse the process from individual perfection to family, tribe, people, nation, and world perfection and rise back to the position that did not fall.  
However, we cannot just rise up. We must fight and win. This is what we refer to in the Unification Church as the restoration through indemnity. To restore, we must fight. We must confront the enemy. We must confront Satan. Even if Satan is dealing with individuals, he represents a cosmic position when dealing with individuals. After winning against Satan, we can then confront the family, tribe, nation, and world, developing victory rights centered on each of these.  
This is how, centered on the history of religion today, although we humans do not know, countless religions in the east, west, south, and north are developing this fight, forming a unified world in the end.  
9  
Religions must transcend material and living realms to take responsibility for the historical process.  
So, what kind of religion will take responsibility for this historical process? What kind of religion must it be? In looking at this issue, it must be a religion that can transcend materiality. Furthermore, it must transcend living realms. It must transcend materiality and living realms. To transcend the living realm, we must overcome and rise above the 'self' connected to that living realm, which is the physical body for us humans. Then, what must happen next? Next, we must leave only God's love, even if it means sacrificing the whole. This is the process we must go through.  
Why is that? If there had been no Fall, all things would have become one centered on God's love, and humanity would have become one. When humanity becomes one, at the same time, it would have formed a unity of love with God, creating a world centered on love, a world centered on love for all things, and a world centered on love for humanity. However, because this was shattered, the central core that lost the historical process must be reapplied to our individual selves, guiding you through that process, which is the path of religion.  
Thus, in the world of religion, what has happened? There has been an era of offerings, a time of offerings. This is about sacrificing all things. It is about striking all things to shed blood. This was the Old Testament era centered on Judaism, which continued for 4,000 years.  
What comes next? The next era is the era of human offerings. It is about striking people. In the New Testament era, when Jesus came to this earth, he became the sacrificial offering on the altar, representing all people, as he bore the cross before the unbelieving nation of Israel. When all things are offered as sacrifices, the sacrificial offering on the altar... When the festival commemorating the first (sacrificial day) is a village event, the entire village bows their heads, or if it is a national event, all the citizens bow their heads. Similarly, when Jesus came to this earth and died on the cross, as he appeared as the substantial offering, all people must bow their heads and obey absolutely to become one with that offering. By becoming one with him, they can receive the benefits of atonement.  
Then, what will happen after this era passes? The next era will be centered on love, whether it is heavenly love or satanic love, leading to the era of offerings. The path that the Unification Church is taking today is not the era of offerings centered on material things, nor is it the era of offerings centered on our substantial selves. It is centered on the issue of love and the issue of family. It is not love centered on a man if he is a man, nor love centered on a woman if she is a woman, nor is the couple just for themselves. The couple represents the whole, the tribe, the nation, and the world. They are a couple for heaven and earth, and even if they must sacrifice all their love, even the love of humanity, they are walking the path to manifest God's love. This is the path of the Unification Church.  
This was the historical mission that religion had to fulfill in today's world. Today, centered on the chosen people of Israel, who inherited the mainstream religions and national thoughts, it signifies the Old Testament era, which, in the terms of the Unification Church today, refers to the era of resurrection. The New Testament era, the era of the covenant, is meant to develop and transcend the world of the end. This is how we see it.  
History has changed due to the Fall, correcting the front and back, left and right, and up and down.  
Historically, it is like this, but when individuals clash with each other in weaving this history, the history of Cain and Abel must inevitably unfold. The fight between the older brother and the younger brother arose due to the Fall. Because the older brother fights the younger brother, the older brother must strike the younger brother. The older brother is the one who came first, and the younger brother came later, so the younger brother stands on God's side while the older brother stands on Satan's side, engaging in the struggle between good and evil.  
What happened because of the Fall? The first shall be last, and the last shall be first. They have been reversed. The up and down have been turned upside down. The one who should stand on the right has stood on the left.  
Therefore, Satan has come to stand on the right. Originally, God should have been on the right, but God has stood on the left and is seeking the right. There will be a history of crossing over. There will be a history of the up and down being reversed. There will come a time in world history when the front and back and left and right will be reversed. That time is what we call the end times.  
Now, looking at it this way, what is the center? What is the standard for the transition to that center? It is not always the individual. It is not the individual. It is the existence of the nation; the nation must always be at the center. Unless we overcome the national standard, we cannot bring about a transitional era. We cannot bring about an era that can change left and right.  
Therefore, God must work to establish a chosen nation on this earth to create the chosen people of Israel. To establish the chosen nation, we must establish the chosen individual, and by establishing the individual, we must create the chosen family, and by creating the family, we must form tribes, peoples, and nations. Through this historical process, we have aimed for gradual development through a long path of suffering.  
So, who was the first to win before God in the history of Israel? As you all know, the word 'Israel' means 'to prevail.' What did they prevail over? They prevailed over the realm of Satan centered on spirit and flesh. In other words, they prevailed over spiritual Satan and substantial Satan. Who was that? It was the family of Jacob. Since there is no time to go into detail, I will just mention the content briefly.  
Thus, they laid the foundation of the clan. By laying this clan foundation and standing on God's side, they must form a national foundation. This is not something that happens within a nation or within a family. The world of Satan is external; therefore, the internal person, the Abel-like existence on God's side, must fight and win against the external world. If they do not have the authority to subdue the external world, they cannot return and establish dominion. It is always a fight.  
Therefore, Jacob, after receiving the blessing that Esau should have received, must go through a suffering course of 21 years, going to the difficult external world of his uncle, being deceived ten times, and suffering greatly, ultimately overcoming and returning victorious. But again, who is in the internal world? Here, the older brother Esau is trying to kill him. He overcame all of that. After acquiring the external victory rights, when returning to the internal world, there was a battle with the spiritual archangel and the substantial older brother—who represents the archangel's side. At the Jabbok River, he fought even as his hip was dislocated and won the name 'Israel,' so when he returned to his hometown, Esau could not strike Jacob. He laid the foundation for unity here.  
Then, where does that victorious tribe go? They must depart for Egypt. They must start to form a nation. So, they go to the enemy nation of Egypt and suffer greatly. After 430 years of hardship, they fought through all that suffering, laid the foundation for victory, and returned to Canaan, but they faced many enemies on their way back to their homeland.  
After overcoming the external enemies, they encounter internal enemies on their journey. Here, centered on faith, centered on God, as families centered on God, tribes centered on God, and nations centered on God, if they had not felt fear from any external forces and had followed God's will directly, Israel would have created national victory rights and formed a nation. However, because humans do not understand this content, they have repeatedly experienced a history of failure.  
Thus, the twelve tribes returned to Canaan, and through many historical processes, they trained the nation of Israel again, awaiting the coming of the Messiah. This is centered on the individual, family, tribe, and nation, focusing on the nation of Israel and Judaism, with the title of the Messiah as a central subject... This is the central being of the nation and the central being of Judaism. If the nation is external, then religion, Judaism is internal; it must send a Messiah who can represent the national victory rights that can complete both the internal and external. Centered on the Messiah, they must become one. When they become one centered on the Messiah, they can represent the victory rights of the internal and external and move again to indemnify centered on the great power of Rome. This historical process of fate cannot be avoided in today's path of restoration through indemnity or the path of restoration. However, due to the death of Jesus, the civilization of Christianity has emerged as the base of Western civilization. Originally, if Jesus had not died...  
The indemnity history that had to be paid due to the death of Jesus  
Centered on Judaism and the nation of Israel, at that time, they were bound by the powerful Roman Empire. At that time, the great power of China in the East would have cooperated to push Jesus against Rome, allowing the nation of Israel, which was caught in between... If the Messiah had come and created the authority to unite the nation of Judah and the twelve tribes of Israel, India and China would have cooperated to push Jesus against Rome. If that had happened, where would the base be? It would not have been a great movement centered on the Roman Empire but rather a movement centered on the Asian Empire, establishing a foundation for unity to oppose Rome. This would have been the providential direction of God's history, but because the nation of Israel did not believe in Jesus and killed him, they lost the foundation of Asia.  
Thus, Christianity entered the external form of the Roman Empire, which it desired as the second paradigm, and had to go through the path of global indemnity. Therefore, Christianity went through a path of suffering for 400 years, and after 400 years, it finally formed a new paradigm centered on the autonomous nation of Christianity, establishing the global paradigm that is today's Christianity.  
In this way, the era of Jesus centered on Judaism was a national standard, but when Jesus came and unified the nation of Israel and Judaism, absorbing the Roman Empire, it should have started from a global perspective, but this was not fully realized.
Because it was not accomplished, we must leave behind this era called the era of the Second Coming and re-establish a new global dominion. The reason for this is that, due to Jesus' death, the spiritual and physical realms were divided. While we only possessed the spiritual Christian ideology, we lost the physical Israelite ideology. This indicates that when Judaism and the nation of Israel looked for the Messiah from a national standard, they had both a nation and religious authority, forming a state with a unified heart and politics. However, today, due to Jesus' death, we find ourselves in a position where spirit and flesh are separated.

The mission and responsibility of the returning Lord
The separation of spirit and flesh means that today the external world and the internal world are divided, leading to a stage where conflict can persist. Therefore, Christianity, which represents the internal world, and numerous nations that represent the external world have always been in a history of struggle. We know that the path of Christianity has left behind a history of unjust and painful bloodshed.

Through this historical process, we have paid the price of individual sacrifices, familial sacrifices, tribal sacrifices, national sacrifices, and the combined sacrifices of numerous nations, forming the spiritual Israelite realm, which we see today as the free world centered around America. 

What will the Lord do when He comes? How will He unify the divided spiritual free world culture into a free world culture centered on both spirit and flesh? In other words, how will He create a unity based on the standards of the nation of Israel and Judaism during the time of Jesus, centered on the global landscape and the foundation of Christianity? This is the mission of the returning Lord.

So, what path must be taken to achieve this unity? The path involves inheriting the legacy from countless spirits who believed in Christianity and came before the Lord. This inheritance must be received, and it is a complex process.

Even if the Messiah is sent to this earth, he must enter the spiritual realm and fight with full authority over heaven and earth, possessing the power to move the entire world. To actualize this, the coming Messiah must integrate the divided spiritual realms. There are numerous spirits, including not only Christians but also Buddhists, Confucians, and many other religious figures, all of whom are divided in the spiritual realm. Therefore, it is essential to unify the divided spiritual realms.

When we look at the spiritual realm, there are groups of Buddhists, Confucians, Muslims, Christians, and many other sects, all of whom present their claims and form cliques in the spiritual realm. This cannot continue.

Originally, within God's will, the spiritual realm is one. If one Adam and Eve had completed their mission and become one with God's love, they would have become true parents, and all spirits who lived on earth through their lineage would be one, belonging to the Adamic lineage. The spiritual realm is also of the Adamic lineage, as is the earthly realm. In other words, the spirits who lived in the Adamic cultural realm and under Adam's dominion reside in the heavenly world. There are no gaps; everything connects.

However, in the spiritual realm, there are numerous groups. For this to unite, individuals cannot come together; it must be at the level of nations and the world, rising to that standard to achieve unity. Because this time has not yet come, all spirits have formed thousands of groups, unable to communicate from east to west. Free movement is impossible.

Today, the world has many borders, and cultural backgrounds are entirely different, making free movement impossible. Similarly, the spiritual realm is in a state of confusion, unable to determine who the subject is, leading to a spiritual realm where individuals assert their claims. Do you understand? 

So how do we unify this? If there are Buddhists, Confucians, or others, they are all asserting their claims in the spiritual realm. Jesus claims his own as well. Therefore, if the returning Lord has a responsibility, what must He do when He appears on earth? He must enter the spiritual world and initiate a movement to unite all these spirits. Do you understand?

To do this, He cannot immediately engage with the spirits. He must rise from the very lowest level of the spiritual realm. To rise, He must first fight against the most wicked Satan. By battling and yielding to the extreme evil of Satan, a spiritual struggle will unfold, leading to division left and right. Only when He overcomes and crosses the boundary can He begin to establish direction; before that, He must win in the midst of the chaotic world of Satan. The place He must win is not just a personal victory but a victory that represents family, tribe, nation, and world. Only after winning in this comprehensive struggle can He enter the spiritual realm and initiate the unification of all.

This is how complex it is. 

So what must the returning Lord do? He must achieve victory over Satan, and then He must achieve victory over all spirits. Today, there are those who boast of being something in the world, but they do not understand how to resolve this fallen realm. Simply hoping and putting in effort is not enough. He must overcome the realm of Satan, and then what must He conquer? He must conquer the realm of the spiritual world. This is not the visible world but the invisible world. If He cannot achieve victory over Satan in the struggle against the invisible world, there will be no path to advance into the spiritual realm. There will always be obstacles, so even if He enters the spiritual realm, He cannot fight and win.

Therefore, possessing the victory over the realm of Satan, He must then enter the spiritual realm with the authority of victory and conquer all the spirits, making Christianity the highest mainstream religion. This means He must inherit all their authority. Through this struggle, when He can receive victorious recognition from heaven and earth, He will be able to begin His practical journey on earth, with God proclaiming, "You are the victor over Satan and the spiritual realm." You must understand this. 

What kind of person is the returning Lord? He must subdue Satan and all the spirits, all the religious leaders, one by one. All must be centered around God's character—because the perfection of God's character is achieved through true love. By centering on God's true love, He must convince everyone of the nature of religion and the universe, leading them to submission.

In other words, all beings in existence wish to be absorbed by the owner of higher love on this earth. Isn't that right? Even the smallest creatures seek out places that can love them more and give to them. The same principle applies.

Therefore, He must subdue them through true love and inherit all their authority. He must inherit the authority of unification. Do you understand? 

This is the responsibility of the Messiah on this earth. It cannot be that only Christianity unites. Even if Christianity can create unity on earth, as long as the cultural backgrounds of Buddhism, Islam, and all other cultures remain as relative foundations, and as long as the boundary remains, it is natural that there can be no unity in the spiritual realm. 

Therefore, He must inherit this authority and manifest it on earth. Do you understand? Today, those who believe in Jesus think He will come on clouds, but in the Unification Church, such nonsense does not exist. There is no such nonsense. People think that just by believing, they will be saved. If it were that simple, why would the founder of the Unification Church take such a difficult path? Why would he make the members suffer, face constant criticism, and opposition? Do you understand?

God's strategy is to take back what was lost.
This struggle to inherit spiritual victory and manifest it on earth is taking place. Do you understand? When the Lord comes to earth, He is not welcomed but is personally attacked by families, tribes, nations, and the entire world. The entire world attacks Him. In this battle, it is not God who attacks first; it is Satan who attacks first. It is from the position where Satan attacks that He must fight back and take back what was lost. Do you understand? He takes back blessings while being attacked.

So how can Abel achieve victory? Cain, after hitting and hitting, eventually thinks, "Oh! I was wrong. That is my brother." This is the history. When Cain cannot continue hitting and becomes aware, he thinks, "Oh! I was wrong," and thus submits. Therefore, God's strategy is to take back what was lost. Satan's strategy is to attack and lose. Do you understand?

Thus, we can see this in our daily lives. What is a good person? What is an evil person? An evil person is one who invades. A good person is one who is invaded. If someone invades a person who is just standing there, the invader is the sinner, right? If someone invades a person who is just standing there, what happens? They will demand compensation for damages. Do you understand? Compensation for damages means if they cause ten damages, they will demand fifteen. This is how compensation is determined.

Therefore, today’s religious people do not understand this strategy. They do not know the strategy of taking back what was lost. It is a simple strategy. Historically, religion has developed when it was persecuted. This is the path that religion must take.

Does that mean that when there is no persecution, religion does not develop? Even without persecution, it can develop. How does it develop? It is when God strikes the believers. It is a time of opposition. If there is no opposition to the Unification Church, then Reverend Moon will make it difficult for the members, making them suffer. If he is blessed by heaven, he will share all that blessing. Do you understand? 

But sharing that blessing does not come without difficulty; he will insult and hit them while sharing. You must be beaten to take the blessings that Reverend Moon possesses. That is how you can take them. The method is simple. Do you understand? 

The method of sharing blessings and receiving blessings…
The way to receive blessings is through the strategy of taking back what was lost. If the religious realm achieves victory, what happens next? The victorious religious leader cannot just sit back. They must strike. The principle is the same. This is how development occurs. If they submit, obey, and give thanks, what happens? They will take all the blessings that the religious leader possesses.

Why do you all want to follow Reverend Moon, who talks so much? There are presidents in this country, presidents in America, and many great religious leaders and scholars in the world. Why do you want to follow Reverend Moon? The answer is simple. It is not anything else. Whether you welcome me or not, the more you make me suffer, the more you will inherit all the blessings that Reverend Moon possesses. 

Therefore, in the end, what does that mean? You are all people who come to take blessings. You are all bad people coming to take blessings. 

The reason for remaining still while being persecuted is because they understood God's strategy.
They did not know that this law applies. It is a simple principle. When you understand the principle, it becomes simple, but it encompasses all decisive elements of victory and defeat in the transformation of heaven and earth. Therefore, will there be welcome on the path that Reverend Moon takes? No. If he carries such a great mission from heaven and earth, there cannot be a welcome. The whole of South Korea opposes him, and even Christianity opposes him. Do you know why? South Korea, Christianity, and even Buddhism have all been against him lately. Even many who worship various deities oppose the Unification Church. 

All the superficial nations, churches, and religions will naturally oppose him. Why? Because they want to gather all the blessings. Do you understand? They want to gather the high blessings, the great blessings, the wide blessings, the flat blessings, the long blessings, and the round blessings; they want to gather all the blessings that have been shared.

Since they are all mixed in a position where they can be invaded by Satan, the way to gather all the blessings from heaven is to let Satan strike and then gather everything as compensation for damages. Do you understand? That is why I have always said that Reverend Moon must face global persecution to fulfill his mission. Only when the whole world opposes him with the intent to kill will our time come.

When a religious leader carrying such a mission comes out of a small valley and causes problems for the nation, Asia, and the world, leading to a total attack, we must recognize that a new historical beginning of God's will can emerge in that era. Do you understand? 

Is it good or bad to be persecuted? "Good." Why does the Unification Church remain still while being persecuted? Why do they remain still? If they hit once, they should hit twice or three times. Why does someone like Reverend Moon remain so miserable and torn yet still stay still? It is not because he is incapable; it is because he understands these things. He knows.
Therefore, does the Unification Church have to perish while being persecuted according to the principle of taking away? "It should prosper!" What does that mean? "It should prosper." It should prosper. It sounds good, doesn't it? Do you understand? When is there no persecution in the external world? It is when the person of the Unification Church, Mr. Moon, has gathered all the blessings of the world and stored them in a warehouse, holding the key to that warehouse. Do you understand? When this happens, there is no opposition. Then where do the thieves come in? They come in here. Where does Satan come in? He comes in here. These bastards! This is about pushing them to their death. That is welcome, unwelcome... Is there a word for unwelcome? Is it approval or disapproval? "It is approval." Those older ladies over there, is it approval or disapproval? They are old and have already suffered enough, and if they persecute the teacher too, they might think, "Oh! When will I ever live comfortably before I die...". So, do the older people approve? "Yes." The grandmothers who came into the Unification Church say, "I entered this church first, hmm, I entered first, so treat me with respect and honor all my ancestors..." (Recording cuts off briefly) These grandmothers! Who are you trying to ruin? They say they won't treat you well. You need to understand that. They are completely taking away the blessings.

Those who do not fully participate here are all being robbed. You need to understand that the people you command and who make your lives difficult have taken away all the blessings you were supposed to receive. In this principle, the struggle between good and evil exists to resolve the fate of restoration through indemnity, and you need to understand that such formulas apply beyond history.

What is the pride of the Unification Church? What is the pride of the Unification Church? "...." What is the pride of the Unification Church? What is the pride of the Unification Church? So, when all this water flows, if it flows from the mountain valley, it should all go to the ocean and form a greater sea, but they have blocked all the dams, the dams. Do you understand? The pride of the Unification Church.

What does the Unification Church mean? What does the 'Unification' in Unification Church mean? "It means 'to unify'." To unify means to lead, right? "It means to lead." What does it mean to lead? Do you understand? "Yes." There are many religious leaders there, but every morning they say, "Good morning!" (Laughter) What does that mean? "Pride." What pride? "The pride of the Unification Church."

Some of you may be hearing this for the first time. So, he is someone who received a seal from the heavenly realm. He came to earth with a divine command and what must he do next? He must fight centered on the five-colored humanity on earth, centered on tribes and nations. Are there no whites, no reds, no yellows, no blacks...? They all fight, whether they are merchants, thieves, or whatever.

So, what happens if they all oppose? If they oppose, what happens? If they all oppose, the Unification Church will have all the second generations come in. Do you understand? It is not the first generation that follows; it is not those who oppose that follow, but the sons and daughters of those who actively opposed who all come in. That is quite a strange strategy, isn't it? Ah, this father is opposing with all his might, but his son becomes a Unification Church member and says, "That old man, that bastard..." (Laughter) That is how it is. The husband is opposing with all his might, but the wife comes in and says, "That bastard husband, that bastard child." (Laughter) And if the wife opposes, the husband says the same. That is the strategy.

Isn't that wonderful? How else could one repay an enemy? The father is an enemy of Mr. Moon, but the son sides with Mr. Moon and is trying to settle the score with the father. So they all foam at the mouth, saying, "Mr. Moon took our sons and daughters. He took our only daughter. He took our only son. He made me so miserable. Boo hoo!" They bark. (Laughter) Can you imagine how noisy the neighborhood is?

Also, when they enter the family, the husbands say, "That bastard Mr. Moon has seduced our wives." And the wives say, "Oh! That bastard Mr. Moon has made my husband go astray. Boo hoo!" They bark. This is how dogs bark in the universe. Can that dog bite even if a thousand dogs bark? Do you understand? Barking is good. Barking means a guest has arrived, it means a guest has arrived! It’s deep here, so it’s a dangerous place. Just a little bit in, and the water suddenly rises, making it a very good place to cause a heart attack. You must be especially careful about that. Usually, kids from the land feel good when they go to the beach. If they like the river and there are fish, they keep trying to catch them and want to catch clams, stepping further in until they suddenly fall in. Moreover, here, it collapses in. If you don’t want to go in, the more you try not to, the further you go in. So you need to be careful about that.

The water is good, and the air is good...

How much of a person is water? "Seven-tenths." It’s three-fourths. A person is a water bag. That’s why people need to drink good water. Moreover, the water here is really good. Just having water isn’t enough. It needs to connect with the air. The air and water must harmonize to be healthy. From that perspective, Cheongpyeong is a really good place.

The teacher has traveled to many countries around the world, but it’s really hard to find a place like this. Korea is a truly beautiful country. I don’t know if you have regretted being born in Korea and wished to be born in another country, but that’s not true. Korea is a truly beautiful country. You haven’t traveled all over the country, right? If you do, you’ll find it’s a really beautiful country. The scenery is beautiful too. Wherever you go, there are beautiful mountains and flowing streams where you can drink. There aren’t many countries like that. You should take pride in being born in Korea. Do you understand that? You must have heard that too. "Yes." That’s the truth.

They say countries like Switzerland are beautiful, but while they are grand and large in scale, they aren’t as mysteriously beautiful as this. You won’t get bored traveling all day in Korea. There’s a lot of change wherever you go. From that perspective, you are receiving the benefits of the natural environment more than any other country in the world. The air is good, there’s sunlight, and the seawater is clear. Clear water flows wherever you go. You can’t see this in most countries.

Think about how good it is for people to have a good environment. The better the environment, the more beautiful people’s thoughts can become. The worse the environment, the less beautiful thoughts can be. That’s why, when looking at Korea’s nature, people are a nation that can think in many ways. Because Korea is exposed to diverse environments, Koreans have a natural talent, a talent given by heaven, to think in various ways.

Also, whether it’s a mountain peak or terrain, everything has a different character. If you look at other countries, the mountain ranges are all connected, but here, regardless of the mountain range, everything shows its unique shape. The fields are unique, and the mountain peaks are unique; everything is unique. Each has a distinct character. Because they grew up in such a natural environment, the personality of Koreans is more unique than that of people from any other country in the world. At the same time, they are independent. They don’t want to listen to anyone and dislike losing to anyone. Even if the peaks are small, they are beautiful in themselves. The environment may be small, but there’s a lot to be proud of. The water is clear, the peaks are clear, the air is clear, and even the bugs... Because they have the environmental conditions to boast of unique characteristics in each region, Koreans born in that environment are uniquely special. Do you understand what I’m saying? "Yes."

But one problem is that the country is small. The Korean Peninsula is a small country, right? The scenery of the three-thousand-ri peninsula is beautiful, but the country is small. Not only is the country small, but now the North and South are divided. The South and North are divided and are in a position of fighting against each other. The South is a country that connects to the democratic world, while the North is a country that connects to the communist world, creating a confrontation with opposing ideologies along the 38th parallel.

When will our Korean people reunite? This is a major task for the future. A nation with strong independence and strong assertions has been divided by communism and democracy for 33 years. A long time has passed, similar to the period under colonial oppression. Those born after liberation are now thirty-three years old. Therefore, having grown up in completely different climates and ideological environments since birth, they have become like people from different countries.

From this perspective, how to digest this and how to unify is the responsibility that the Korean people must bear in the future. However, both the South Korean and North Korean peoples are very assertive... Even from a communist perspective, the most vicious and terrifying communists are in North Korea.

Also, even in the democratic world, whether in America or any other country, they are adventurous, acting like a small group that creates chaos, always walking at the forefront of trends. Even on the international stage, the Korean people do not fall behind. They are a unique nation.

With such a unique character, how can the South and North become one? I think there will be great difficulties ahead in unifying. That’s why I believe education alone will be difficult. So, it must be done with a special ideology. What kind of ideology? It cannot be an ideology that asserts power. It must be an ideology that creates unity through love.

The Unification Church is an organization that carries a global ideology centered on God. So, within that context, God must have created the Unification Church because He loves Korea. Although there are unique characters, they can unite under the ‘will’. It is through the power of loving centered on that will that they can become one. Therefore, in the future, South Korea must have the subjectivity of an ideology centered on that love. Without that, I believe there will be no day when this nation can become one. If the divided North and South can be completely unified into a love-centered system, then unifying the world’s nations will not be a problem. Do you understand what I’m saying?

What does our Unification Church carry as its meaning? It carries a global ideology centered on God. It is not an ethnic ideology. It is not an ideology focused on the Republic of Korea. It carries a great ideology centered on heaven and earth. This ideology is the mainstream.

Love, within love, includes loving parents... To love parents, one must know how to love siblings. Also, a person who knows how to love siblings can love parents. Parents naturally love children who love their siblings more. It works like this. One must know how to love parents, then know how to love siblings, and then know how to love relatives. You have uncles, cousins, and so on, right? You must not fight with those relatives but unite and love each other. Then, you must love your neighbors. When that expands, it becomes a societal issue, then a national issue, and then a global issue. As the scope expands, it becomes increasingly bleak. Love tends to thin out, and how should I say, love gradually disappears. That cannot happen. As time goes on, love must grow stronger. Do you understand what I’m saying? The path to finding love that can grow stronger as time goes on is the path where one can meet God and connect with God through love.

Until now, when we say ‘love’, the distant things become increasingly unrelated, and it has all been concentrated on my mother, father, and siblings. It has all borne fruit within the family centered around me, such as my husband or wife. It has all been wrapped up in that. That is the family of the fallen world until now.

What makes our Unification Church different is this. What is the Unification Church? It is to love siblings as one loves parents, to love tribes as one loves siblings, to love nations, and to love the world. It is to love the nation even if it means abandoning parents. To love the world, one must be willing to abandon their own country. Furthermore, to love heaven, one must be willing to abandon the world. It is the path of love that seeks to sacrifice the close and small for the distant and great. This is the main ideology of the Unification Church. It’s simple. Do you understand?

But what kind of ideology is that? It is not the ideology of the teacher. It is not the ideology of Reverend Moon as spoken of in America. If we were to say it in the way it is spoken here, it is not the teacher’s ideology. That ideology is originally God’s ideology. When we look at what kind of being God is, He is the one who loves the other more than Himself. He loves the other more than Himself so that two people can unite and love a larger scope of the other. That is God’s movement. Because God’s ideology is fundamentally this, He sends the person closest to Him into the evil world to sacrifice for humanity. That is God’s ideology.

Therefore, historical figures, saints, and wise men who have come and gone in the past all came to this world with the title of ‘Let’s love humanity’. Such people did not focus on loving their own families. They loved nations and the world. They loved beyond nations to the world. And rather than being welcomed, they were all rejected and sacrificed.

As that era draws closer, we have finally begun to honor those who have been sacrificed and those who have upheld such ideologies. Those figures are like Jesus Christ today, the founders of religions. People like Jesus, Buddha, and Confucius are all such figures. Isn’t that right?

What is their ideology? It is not just for their own families. It is to create one family for the universe... To establish the family of the universe, one must sacrifice all lower systems, such as nations, tribes, ethnicities, families, and individuals. That is the difference. Do you understand? 

Worldly love is all about being tied to our home, our mom and dad, but God’s love is based on this and jumps beyond it. In terms of the Old and New Testament ideologies, it means that to gain the greater, one must make the lesser a sacrifice.

That’s why to walk the good path, one must make sacrifices. What is sacrifice? It is to become a offering. What is an offering? It is to shed blood and sweat and to stand in the position of giving oneself up. If we were to express this in the language of the Unification Church, it means that without going through the process of restoration through indemnity, the expectation of goodness cannot be established. Do you understand?

For the expectation of family goodness to be established, the family must become an offering for the tribe. Without that, the expectation of family goodness cannot be established. Do you understand? Furthermore, for the expectation of tribal goodness to be established, one must become an offering for the nation. It’s a step down. The path of justice that restarted from leaving Heungnam Prison
As the association president just mentioned, as we meet today, I think of this day in 1950. When I think of this day, which marks the 28th anniversary, I feel that time flies. Time flies, and I have this feeling. It feels like just yesterday, just yesterday. It has already been 28 years, but it feels like just yesterday.

At that time, there was no Unification Church itself, and the teacher came down alone, a solitary figure, from the North to the South. That time feels like just yesterday, but that period that feels like just yesterday has become 28 years. Many dream-like stories have arisen during that time. The Unification Church laid its foundation in Korea, then passed through Japan to America, and now has emerged as a problematic group, a problematic religious organization, all within this short, dream-like 28-year period.

On October 14, 1978 (Saturday), at the Cheonseong Mountain Holy Ground (Cheongpyeong).
* This statement was made during the 28th anniversary ceremony of the release from Heungnam Prison, and the title was added by the editor.

When I think about it, how old was the teacher at that time? Now, at 58 years old, how old was he then? "30 years old." 30 years old. At 30, he was a young man, right? Let’s see how many people here are 30 years old. How many are there? 30 years old. There are not many here. How about those under 30? There should be many. At 30, it is quite young. At that time, compared to now, the teacher was quite young, and when he came out of prison, what was his resolution? It was a restart, a restart. No matter how much hardship he faced in North Korea, he forgot all the difficulties there, and that difficult fact did not bring him loss on the path he was going but rather served as a stimulus for his second start. That was the age he was at.

So, crossing the 38th parallel and going down… If I were to talk about that, it would take a long time. He came down to South Korea… It took about 2 months to reach Busan after passing through Gyeongju. When he arrived in Busan, he found that the refugees were packed, and there was no place to hide. So, he had no choice but to dig a cave and live as a refugee.

During that period, in order to live independently as a human being, he had to solve economic problems and various issues on his own, so he did all sorts of work. You all know that when it comes to Teacher Moon, you think of him as a great person, but I can do anything. When I go to the labor market, I become a laborer, and if I go to a factory, I become a worker. I have a lot of such experiences. When I go to the seaside, I become a sailor, and when I go to the mountains, I become a mountain man. It’s about adaptability. I have a lot of qualities that allow me to adapt to the environment. It’s a trained quality rather than a natural one. Without becoming an independent subject who can survive in any environment through self-training, one cannot fulfill such a tremendous great purpose.

If one’s academic path is blocked by opposition, and one cannot achieve their purpose in that path, then one must take the opposite path, the opposite path. If one cannot achieve their purpose even by taking the opposite path, then they must take another path… I felt a sense of responsibility that I must not fail to complete the path of purpose by any means, so in the body of a young man in his 30s who came out of prison, there was a strong resolution to start anew. It feels like just yesterday.

The 1960s, when I faced the most opposition from everyone
There are many stories behind that. While being pursued by the Chinese army, crossing mountains and fields to reach the front line, there were many stories, but in the end, heaven protected me, and I came to South Korea. Even in South Korea, those from Busan, especially from Beomeo-dong, know that I built a cave there and was preparing for a second start.

At that time, there was the issue of evangelizing the established church… At that time, Evangelist Kang Hyun-sil came in. In that way, heaven sent one person, then another, who shared the same purpose, and we gathered again to present the issues of South Korea, laying the foundation for the Unification Church, which was established and completed the national standard by the 1970s, stepping onto a new global stage. Do you know how much a person with a temperament like the teacher has gritted their teeth and bitten their tongue to endure? "The coming night is the enemy. I must go. The evening coming is the enemy! I must start work in the morning, but the night coming is the enemy." This was the mindset we had.

We could not help but rise up as a brotherly kingdom, breaking away from the position of Korea. Therefore, the teacher expanded the global landscape that could subdue the eldest son centered around the country of America, but you must understand that you need a conditional foundation. Do you understand? "Yes."

So what is the home church I mentioned earlier? It represents the whole. It represents all families, all of this. Do you understand? "Yes." This is how it has become, but how has it turned out? It has all come together, and how has it happened? It has all been sewn up, and it has become something like this. Do you understand? "Yes." And it has not attached itself here.

Regarding home church activities, after this standard has all been established... Do you understand what I mean? "Yes." The entire landscape of global victory has been reduced to a minimum unit, which is a single altar. Do you understand? Do you understand what I mean?

This 360 families represent the 360 tribes of the world, and 360 refers to time, and 360 degrees refers to space, thus referring to time and space. Time and space combined symbolize the whole. That is why it is the number 360. Also, the number 360 is the multiple of 3 and 4, which is 12, and 12 is multiplied by 3. What is 12? It refers to the national... The Old Testament, the New Testament, and the Age of the Divine Principle all revolve around the number 12, passing through three eras... It is also an expanded number of 36. Do you understand? It refers to a vertical time and space. Also, twelve months in a year is 360 days. It refers to the many days of the restoration era. Those days have failed. Because of the failure of one day, one year, ten years, one hundred years, and one thousand years have all been eroded. Do you understand what I mean? If those days succeed, those days will be resurrected. It refers to the resurrection of all the days of world history that have passed until now.

Next, the number of nations, 360, refers to Cain representing the world. The Cain world that represents the world remains before you. What does the number 360 mean? What does the home church mean? It means that the Cain world stands in the position of the eldest son representing the world. To become heaven, you must subdue the elder brother as Abel, as the younger brother. Therefore, without restoring the rights of the eldest son, you cannot serve the parents. Do you understand? "Yes." Do you understand or not? You must understand. Because Cain was born in the position of the eldest son due to the fall, to resolve this, you must subdue the rights of the eldest son representing the world from the position of the younger son. It must be subdued all at once. Based on a foundation of three years or three and a half years, there is a need to shorten it.

To say to do home church is to provide the gospel that gives unspeakable brightness and hope. But what time is it now? You are on the foundation of victory that the teacher has established centered around global conditions, so you must inherit the teacher's heart. You must be able to say, "I am undoubtedly the son or daughter of the True Parents, and I was born in the Abel position, but I will surely subdue the Cain stage of this world." Why? Because in the spiritual realm, the foundation of complete victory has been laid, and the power of the substantial realm will go out and will be pushed back. You must do it with confidence. Do you understand what I mean?

Therefore, during this period, the teacher is moving from the position of the servant of servants, to the position of the servant, from the position of the servant to the position of the adopted son, and from the position of the adopted son to the position of the son, and is representing the position of the parents. This is the foundation of home church activities. In other words, it is an altar that can simultaneously indemnify all historical aspects of the restoration of the rights of the eldest son before God in the historical era. You must understand that the name home church in the Unification Church has laid the foundation for the decisive resolution of heaven and hell on this earth, which is revolutionary and amazing. You must understand that this is the word of the gospel that brings unspeakable brightness and hope in the historical era of blood.

Hearing this word and saying, "Oh, what is home church again?" is not acceptable. The Unification Church is filled with hope, regretting what they could not take responsibility for in the past, and pledging new resolutions and determination to settle the past life that left sorrow before heaven through the historical process of home church, and to digest all the satanic rights that have violated today's era with my own fist and body, and to boldly start with the conviction that we will do so. You must understand this. Do you understand? "Yes."

After subduing everything centered on the individual, you must subdue the family. For three and a half years, you cannot go to your family. For three and a half years, whether you are a man or a woman, you must devote yourselves... If all men with families are doing this, the people in the neighborhood will say, "Quickly bring your wife," and they will prepare everything for living, so that you will not have to worry about food, and you can bring your wife. Do you understand? "Yes." If the wife goes and is putting in her effort to establish a foundation, the people there will all say, "If you have a husband, bring your husband to our area. If you have any difficulties with your household, we can take full responsibility for everything, so please bring him." This is how it should be.

When they meet, that place becomes their tribal realm. Therefore, if you look, there are two houses, the husband and wife, two places... If each has 360 houses, that makes 720 houses. Right? 720 houses will automatically form a familial tribal realm centered around the couple. Wherever the two people go, they will naturally be welcomed, and in all the paths they take, they will inherit your traditional thoughts. When it is undoubtedly concluded that they have all come, a great movement of the new Israel heavenly kingdom will unfold. Therefore, they will move from that tribe towards the nation. Do you understand?

Once recognized by the nation, a tribal messiah realm will be established, and centered around the family, the Buddhas can return to their hometowns and create a tribal messiah realm. When entering the family, as soon as you enter, you become one. There is no need to worry about the family.

The same goes for forming a tribe with God. God has sent out the closest sons and daughters until now, and when they achieve victory, He has worked to bring them back to Himself. Do you understand? That is why He has chosen the closest people. Is that right or not? "That's right."

Thus, the external Cain rights and the internal Cain rights—your own lineage—must unite for the Cain and Abel tribal rights to finally become one. Because of this, you can reign in the position of the Messiah and finally receive your wife and children, becoming the True Parents. You must clearly understand this.

However, before loving your own sons and daughters, you must love the children of the Satanic side on this fallen earth. Without establishing the condition of having loved the children of the Satanic side, you cannot love your own children. The teacher also had such a destiny, so he abandoned all his children and packed his belongings to head north of the 38th parallel. He had to establish the condition of having loved many people in the enemy's nation and could not return without doing so. Therefore, he had to subdue the enemy's nation and return.

This is the path of destiny for individuals, families, tribes, nations, and the world, so the Messiah comes out to lay the foundation of victory on behalf of the whole. The person who can lay this foundation becomes the center, and you go on by reducing the global victory that he has achieved. You will shorten the 30-year history into three years. Do you understand? Since liberation until this year, it has been 33 years. Right? "Yes." It has been 33 years in the Unification Church.

Therefore, it is the time to overcome the national dimension of the era that can resolve the resentment of Jesus, and that is why today the Republic of Korea welcomes the teacher's return. Do you understand? "Yes." Even if the established church opposes it, many people will arise in the future to fight on behalf of the Unification Church in the Republic of Korea. Do you think that will happen?

God commanded home church to prevent becoming a fallen soldier. Now, all of you in the Unification Church families must unite completely... In the Republic of Korea itself, the North is Cain, and the South is Abel. Therefore, the South must completely unite in front of the will and stand in a position to digest all of the North centered around Kim Il-sung. When the nation stands on this traditional love, it means that in the future, you can press the button at will. It is when you can do that that you will enter. Do you understand? When we reach the extended era of three and a half years after the end of the third seven-year course, and surpass 1984, no matter how much Kim Il-sung jumps around, we will enter an era where we can say, "Why is this child acting like this?" and suppress him. Do you understand?

Here, you must have the bright national spirit that can spread to the world, and know that the time is not far when all people can raise their banners high and sound the trumpets of marching, and that you must be busier preparing for that from now on. If you cannot keep up with this, you will surely become a fallen soldier. Do you understand or not? "I understand." Therefore, to prevent becoming a fallen soldier, the teacher commanded you to do home church.

Thus, you must become tribal messiahs and enter heaven. By indemnifying the tribal foundation that Jesus could not achieve, you will naturally connect the victorious foundation of the national foundation you have established with the world and proceed directly to heaven through a development stage without persecution. Now, the era of persecution of the Unification Church is passing, right? "Yes." It will end with the third seven-year course. No matter how much America does this or that, it is all coming to an end now. Do you understand? "Yes."

So now, knowing that our era is near, you must return to your families and become a model and exemplary family before this nation... The 777 families have such a mission, so you must be a model. Also, considering the age, you are in your 30s, right? How old are you? "In my 30s." How old are you now? "Thirty-one." You are under thirty-three years old. I see it this way. Therefore, the 777 families must stand in that position and take the lead. Do you understand or not? "I understand." You should not follow the older brothers of the past. We are in a new place... Now, we are inviting children as well. In the past, older brother families would lay the children down and work, but you must carry the children around. Why? For home church... Sounds good, doesn't it? "Sounds good!"

Everyone, there is a satellite base, right? At Cape Kennedy. It goes "bang!" and flies to the moon and to heaven. Because of home church, your lineage can fly. Do you understand? You must have a base to fly to heaven. The teacher can fly for the world, but you do not have a base, right?

That is why you must be grafted in. You must be grafted into the world, and home church must become like a round tomb, growing, maturing, and completing, and then flying away... Also, when determining that home church... Although the Republic of Korea is here, if you say, "I am going to Africa now," you must go to Africa and restore 360 families there. What does that mean? It means transcending borders and transcending nations. Do you understand? "Yes." The time will come when that can happen. 

This means that even if the whole world opposes the Unification Church and the teacher, if one country in Africa welcomes the teacher, it means that from there, the world can be restored. Numerous countries like the nation of John the Baptist will arise. Do you understand?

To win in home church, you must first enter the position of a servant. Because God's will is like this, the restoration history until now has all been concentrated through one thing. It is an amazing fact that we have laid the foundation to march in the midst of a bright light that shines brighter than day, like a new flare, having broken through and established a base in the satanic world. Now, is this home church march difficult? You must traverse the six continents and cross the five oceans to restore...
I need to resolve my resentment... Nowadays, you can see the whole world in front of your eyes, 
you can operate on a stage where you can go anywhere within three hours, and even if you hold 
on and fight freely, you can do so in an environment where the language is not different. 
Can't you lay the foundation for home church victory? If you can't, you will perish. 
You will perish. You will perish! 
First, you need to go to the kitchen every day as a servant and offer a sacrifice. 
When Sunday and Saturday come, you change your clothes and offer a sacrifice. 
It's fine even if you wear a suit. You all need to offer sacrifices. It starts from being a servant. 
Then you rise from being a servant. This is restoration. After doing this for a few months, 
you will say, "Ah, let's stop now. We will do it." Those who were just sitting around, sleeping, 
or acting dirty will all pick up brooms and step forward first. Such a game will unfold. 
It will definitely change. You will find it unbearable not to work when you come in to work. 
What you do will be changed in return. Just wait and see. You will see it with your own eyes. 
It's really wonderful.
You rise from the position of a servant to the position of a servant, and then what? 
You rise to the position of an adopted child. And then? You rise from the position of an adopted child to the position of a direct child. 
To do that, you must lead even the prodigal son. If you do not make everyone submit to the home church foundation, 
you cannot rise to the position of a direct child. Do you understand?
Whether you go to heaven or not is determined by the stage of your actual activities. 
Such a fact has never existed in history. That is why this is the truth, and when you think of this place as 
the place where people seeking heaven will go in the future... the Unification Church does not need the word evangelism. 
If you want to go, go; if you don't want to go, don't. On days when you don't go... after placing all 360 homes in 
the Republic of Korea, you must go to Manchuria, go to Siberia, go to Japan, or cross the Pacific or Africa to find home churches. 
Such a great migration is bound to happen. Do you understand? 
Those who opposed the Unification Church in established churches will see. In the era when home churches are established in Korea, 
they will have to pack their bags and go to North Manchuria and Siberia. They must voluntarily seek the path of sacrifice. 
They must turn their backs on their nation, their blood relatives, and their clans. Those who opposed and persecuted 
the path that True Father of the Unification Church walked today will all go and be persecuted before foreign nations, 
suffering in front of foreign nations, and must find a way to live through foreign nations. Do you understand?
If you cannot do this, even the members of the Unification Church, even the blessed people, will all have to pack their bags and go. 
At that time, they will be out of the blessing. Therefore, whether you complete it centered on the home church foundation or not, 
from now on, the genealogy of the Unification Church will be established. Do you understand? "Yes." 
Centered on the Unification Church teacher, centered on the parents, those who laid the foundation of victory in the home church, 
will organize the genealogy centered on those who became the heirs of the firstborn's enterprise. 
Have you risen in the genealogy or not? "I have." What do you mean you have risen? It's on hold, on hold. 
The paperwork has not been processed. 
You cannot rise in the genealogy until you inherit the firstborn's enterprise and establish a heart of filial piety before your parents. 
Can a second son rise in the heavenly genealogy? No, he cannot. However, a second son in the position of the firstborn will rise in the genealogy. 
The people in your home church area may not know anything, but those who submit to you will unconditionally be blessed. 
Rather, a person who did not believe in religion in the past, who is not an established church member, who is not a Buddhist, 
and who was not a member of another religion, will be blessed for not opposing the Unification Church because they did not know anything.
Did you not know that it would be judged so strangely? Did you know or not? "I did not know." 
When that happens, all the blessings that the teacher receives will become your blessings. 
Now, if you plant trees from there, they will grow vigorously and spread to the world, and when the best seeds come out, 
each country will take those seeds. Do you understand? Do you want to leave bad seeds or good seeds? 
Can you leave good seeds while fighting and growling every day? When you love each other, care for each other, 
the flowers of peace bloom, and the fragrance of love spreads, that place will become the foundation of joy for the whole world 
and an object of reverence. Is this what the Unification Church members who act like jumping frogs today call heaven? 
I do not want such a heaven. No matter how many cows you kill and invite me to a feast, I will not go to such a place. 
Do you understand or not? "I understand." Did you understand for sure or not? "I understood." 
To complete the firstborn's enterprise, the home church must be done.
So, would you like to try visiting? "Yes." Where to? "To the home church...." Home church! 
How many pairs of shoes will you drop? If you have lived for 30 years, you must drop more than 30 years' worth of shoes. 
360 homes mean more than 12 countries. It is the same as more than 12 countries. There are all kinds of clans there. 
When it comes to putting your heart into it, if there are people who believe in religion among those 360 homes, 
you must be ahead of any religious believer. You must be ahead of anyone who shows filial piety. 
If there was someone who became a loyal subject, you must be ahead of that loyal subject, ahead of any descendants. 
Only then can you establish a family that builds prestige, knowing that you must act based on justice day and night... 
You cannot do it casually.
Heaven will remember everything. Now, your history centered on each home church will be recorded in heaven. 
Until now, everyone was a refugee and a wandering group, so it was not a sin to go to someone else's house and eat when hungry. 
In a refugee situation, it is like that, right? In a refugee situation, even if you carry several sacks of rice while the owner is watching when you are hungry, 
the owner cannot oppose it. However, you cannot do that from now on. From now on, the problem is different. 
You must establish a tradition as a substantial action and living stage that can eternally establish the law of justice based on the heavenly principle. 
You must clearly understand that this is the responsibility you must take as you seek the home church. Do you understand or not? 
"I understand." Even if you teach this and you cannot do it, I will not take responsibility.
Knowing this, the teacher has also come this far. If you move centered on the home church for just three years, 
you will know who the communists are. You will know who is who. More than any police or anyone else... 
If you act centered on the hope of the home church, as True Father and God love, you will become a second God. 
In knowing, you are a second God, in serving, you are a second God, in showing filial piety, you are a second God, 
in any work, in any activity, you will become a second God. Standing in such a position, I wish you to have a shining home church stage. 
Do you understand? "Yes."
So, will you do it or not? "I will." If you will, say 'Amen!' "Amen." What is 'Amen!'? 
Call out to God and the earth loudly while saying 'A-a-men!' "A-a-men!" You listen well! (Laughter) 
Did you understand home church? "Yes." Why do we need to do it? To complete the firstborn's enterprise.... 
Do you understand? If you stand in the position of a second son, you cannot receive the inheritance. 
You cannot receive the enterprise. Right? There is a firstborn, and can a second son inherit the enterprise? No, he cannot. 
Who inherits it? "The firstborn." The firstborn! Why do we need the firstborn? To receive the inheritance of the heavenly principle.... 
The position of a second son, the Abel-like position, cannot do it. 
To inherit the firstborn's enterprise, stand at the forefront of home church activities.
So, do you want to inherit the heavenly principle? "Yes." On the day you inherit it, God becomes mine, 
the archangel becomes mine, all creation becomes mine, humanity becomes mine, and everything dances in my love, in my love. 
Just like everything dances in God's love, it dances in my love. Right? If you have received the heavenly principle, 
the heir who has received it will rejoice, and if he is sad, everyone will be sad, right? "Yes." 
You must understand that there is no way to live without going through him. 
That is why the way of the home church is the way of inevitable destiny. This is destiny, it is a born fate. 
Do not think sadly that you have become the Unification Church food that cannot go the way of destiny, 
but think gloriously and go out proudly! "A-men!" 
Then, you will receive 100 percent of everything that the teacher has cultivated for his entire life, for 60 years. 
When you complete that, if the teacher is in the heavenly palace, you will be able to connect with the palace and go anywhere. 
The rights of all people as brothers of equality and the privileges of being children of God are a blessed pouch shared by all people. 
Do you understand? What kind of place is it? "A pouch of blessings." Don't mess it up. 
You will get caught immediately. This is not a game of the world. 
Do you understand?
When you come to know this principle, you must go day and night without resting for 24 hours. 
Unification Church members are busy on their way. In a life where you do not know when you will die, 
can you eat without doing this? You cannot rest. All spirits are cooperating with me. 
When I sleep, they wake me up saying, "You brat!" My ancestors do not let me sleep and tell me to work day and night. 
All the spirits on that stage, whether they are Buddhist spirits or good ancestral spirits, all say, "Come back." 
When they say that, it comes like lightning. They cannot come because they cannot come. Do you understand? 
Now, when it comes, it does not go. In the past, when it came, it had to work for a day and return, 
but now, on the day it comes, it can stay without going.
So, there will be a change in an instant. The darkness will brighten, and a dangerous new morning will come to the satanic world, 
an explosive new morning. "I thought there was only one Messiah, but now thousands of Messiah situations have erupted!" 
Just thinking about this feels good, doesn't it? "Yes, it feels good." 
Are you going to stir things up nicely? "Yes." You should slap some of them. 
When will the resentment of being slapped in the past be resolved? Even when I die, I cannot resolve the resentment of being slapped, 
but I can resolve all the resentment of being slapped within a few years. 
And now, the time has come when I can live while shaking my tail in front of my eyes, 
crying tears like chicken droppings, just asking to be saved.
You must know that the dawn of hope for the future of unification is breaking. 
Do you understand? "Yes." If there is a high mountain that hinders the dawn, 
you must tear down that mountain. You must understand that this is what home church activities are for. 
Now, did the mothers of babies understand or not? "I understood." Did the fathers of babies understand or not? 
"I understood." Now, do you have to choose to go to the home church or not? "I will go." 
What about the baby? "I will carry him." What if he cries? 
It’s okay to carry him upside down. It’s fine to drag him along, wrapped in a blanket.... 
Isn't that better than being taken away by the satanic world?
Today, you have gathered here and listened clearly, so go and talk in your local areas. 
The 777 families have heard it first, so you go and talk nationwide. 
Go around the country and light a fire saying, "The teacher said this." 
Do you understand? "Yes." Then, that means the teacher does not have to go on a tour anymore. 
Right? "Yes." I promised. I do not have time to go on a tour. 
You must go back and, as representatives, sweat and convey these words instead of the teacher. 
I sincerely hope that you become the 777 families who can light a fire for everyone! 
"Amen!" It is not you who say 'Amen!' I must say 'Amen!' 
A-men! Then you say it. Since I said 'Amen!'.... "A-men!" 
That’s how it should be. Are you saying 'Amen!' without knowing the order? (Laughter) 
Now you understand about home church, right? "Yes." Why? "To receive the firstborn's enterprise...." 
What must happen to receive the firstborn's enterprise? You cannot receive the enterprise from the position of a second son. 
That is why you must understand the humble historical era of Abel well. 
Since you have not received more than that, you must come before the heavenly principle with the body of the firstborn 
to solely inherit that enterprise. You must understand that the time has come for that. 
The time of religion has come. The time of the Unification Church has come. Did you understand clearly? "Yes."
Satan did not know it would turn out like this. 
He did not know that a person named Moon would appear and completely destroy the satanic world. 
He has completely destroyed the satanic world, right? 
He has broken it all into pieces so that it cannot be patched up.
Now, let's diligently create and shape a new heaven from here. 
Will it be joyful or sorrowful? "Joyful!" The satanic world will be sorrowful, but how about heaven? 
"It will not be sorrowful!" How about you? "It will be good!" It will be good! (Laughter)
So, knowing that, you have made all the promises. "Yes." 
If you are going to work hard until you die, sing and meditate. 
If you create home churches and contact me, I will give you the blessing. 
Do you want me to bless you first? "Please bless me so I can start."
